**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Firefox CSS calc() Value Overflow

## Your Task

Firefox crashes when processing CSS calc() with extreme values. Find the C++ source files in mozilla/gecko-dev that (1) parse CSS calc() expressions and (2) handle numeric overflow during calc() value resolution.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

   - `servo/components/style/values/computed/length_percentage.rs` - The `new_calc()` function uses `AllowedNumericType` for clamping

The key files for the task are:
1. `servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs` - Parses CSS calc() expressions
2. `servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs` - Handles numeric overflow during calc() value resolution (via `simplify_and_sort_direct_children()` which handles NaN, infinity, etc.)
3. `servo/components/style_traits/values.rs` - Defines `AllowedNumericType` with `clamp()` for overflow handling

452026-03-11T02:56:23.984631agentmessage-
The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

The Firefox codebase (gecko-dev mirror at `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8`) uses **Rust (Servo)** for CSS parsing, not C++. The relevant source files are:

### 1. CSS calc() Parsing
**`servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs`** — The primary calc() parser:
- `MathFunction` enum: All supported math functions (calc, min, max, clamp, round, mod, rem, sin, cos, tan, etc.)
- `Leaf` enum: Leaf node types (Length, Angle, Time, Percentage, Number, etc.)
- `CalcNode::parse()`: Top-level parser dispatching to sub-parsers
- `CalcNode::parse_one()`: Parses individual tokens (dimensions, numbers, percentages, nested functions)
- Convenience functions: `parse_length_or_percentage()`, `parse_length()`, `parse_number()`, etc.

### 2. Numeric Overflow Handling
**`servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs`** — Resolution and overflow:
- `GenericCalcNode`: The generic AST node
- `simplify_and_sort_direct_children()`: CSS calc simplification with NaN/infinity handling
- `resolve_internal()`: Evaluates calc expressions, handles NaN propagation, infinity arithmetic, and special cases for round/mod/rem with extreme values

**`servo/components/style_traits/values.rs`** — Clamping mechanism:
- `AllowedNumericType`: Controls post-resolution clamping (`All`, `NonNegative`, `AtLeastOne`, `ZeroToOne`)
- `AllowedNumericType::clamp()`: Applies clamping to handle overflow (e.g., extreme values get clamped to property-specific limits)

To summarize what I found:

The Firefox codebase (gecko-dev mirror) implements CSS calc() parsing and numeric overflow handling in **Rust (Servo)** source files:

1. **`servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs`** — Parses CSS calc() expressions:
   - `MathFunction` enum (calc, min, max, clamp, round, mod, rem, sin, cos, tan, etc.)
   - `Leaf` enum (Length, Angle, Time, Percentage, Number, etc.)
   - `CalcNode::parse()` — top-level parser
   - `CalcNode::parse_one()` — parses individual tokens
   - Convenience parsers: `parse_length_or_percentage()`, `parse_length()`, `parse_number()`, etc.

2. **`servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs`** — Handles numeric overflow during calc() resolution:
   - `GenericCalcNode` — the generic AST node
   - `simplify_and_sort_direct_children()` — implements CSS calc simplification with NaN/infinity handling
   - `resolve_internal()` — evaluates calc expressions, handles NaN propagation, infinity arithmetic, and special cases for extreme values

3. **`servo/components/style_traits/values.rs`** — Defines the overflow clamping mechanism:
   - `AllowedNumericType` enum (`All`, `NonNegative`, `AtLeastOne`, `ZeroToOne`)
   - `AllowedNumericType::clamp()` — clamps resolved values to property-specific limits to handle overflow
